CREATE TABLE webappsstore (domain TEXT, key TEXT, value TEXT, secure INTEGER, owner TEXT)
CREATE UNIQUE INDEX webappsstore_tmp  ON webappsstore(domain, key)
INSERT OR IGNORE INTO webappsstore(domain, key, value, secure, owner) SELECT domain, key, value, secure, domain FROM moz_webappsstore
SELECT key, secure FROM webappsstore WHERE domain = ?1
SELECT value, secure, owner FROM webappsstore WHERE domain = ?1 AND key = ?2
INSERT INTO webappsstore(domain, key, value, secure, owner) VALUES (?1, ?2, ?3, ?4, ?5)
UPDATE webappsstore SET value = ?1, secure = ?2, owner = ?3WHERE domain = ?4 AND key = ?5 
UPDATE webappsstore SET secure = ?1 WHERE domain = ?2 AND key = ?3 
DELETE FROM webappsstore WHERE domain = ?1 AND key = ?2
SELECT SUM(LENGTH(key) + LENGTH(value)) FROM webappsstore WHERE owner = ?1
